Club X Xenia Tornado Memorial - Club X Soccer

04/30/2016 - 05/01/2016  -  Xenia, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15,U16,U17,U18,U19
Girls: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15,U16,U17,U18,U19

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: Applications are considered from youth teams which are properly registered. Players must be currently registered with a team by their State or Provincial association. Each team coach or manager must be able to produce their USYSA (USSF for senior players) player pass or it's equivalent from the Federation affiliated association for each player. U8,U9 and U10 teams may have a maximum of 12 players on their roster. U11 and U12 teams may have a maximum of 14 players on their roster. U13 thru U19 may have a maximum of 18 players on their roster. For U-16 and older teams, a maximum of 22 players may be carded but only 18 may dress for any match on the sideline. No player may play on more than one team during the tournament. U8 teams may use up to 3 guest players, U9-U19 may use up to 4 guest players. No guest player may play on more than one team in the tournament or be rostered to more than one team.

Archived Website: http://www.clubxtornado.com/

Gender: Male Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15,U16,U17,U18,U19
Girls: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15,U16,U17,U18,U19

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: We invite you to join us for the 38th NOSO Cup International Youth Soccer Tournament hosted by the North Olmsted Soccer Organization, July 4th-5th, 2015. Located in a suburb of Cleveland, Ohio, the tournament takes place over the July 4th holiday and is played over two days with each team guaranteed 3 games.
The Tournament is open to boys and girls teams in the U8 through U19 age groups and includes two divisions: the Cup Division is our top division for premier, club and top division travel teams; and the Trophy Division, our lower division for travel teams and competitive recreational clubs. Winning teams in both divisions will receive awards and individual awards will be given to champions and finalists except in the U8 and U9 age groups where participation awards will be given.
Many teams use the tournament as a link between the spring and fall sessions - a last get together for teams having completed the spring season, or a first get together for teams competing in the fall.
Since 1977, teams from throughout the Midwest and as far away as Minnesota, Florida and Texas have participated. International teams have come from Canada, the United Kingdom, Germany and France.
In addition to the tournament, northern Ohio is home to an exciting lineup of attractions that includes the Rock and Roll Hall of Fame and Cedar Point Amusement Park. Make a vacation out of the tournament, come for the competition and stay for the wide variety of activities!

For further tournament information, contact us at info@nosocup.org

Archived Website: http://www.NOSOCup.org

Gender: Male    Age Group(s):  Boys: U14,U15,U16,U17,U18,U19
Girls: U14,U15,U16,U17,U18,U19

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: The Ohio High School Summer Soccer Challenge is coming! The Summer Soccer Challenge is a one day preseason tournament on Saturday, July 11 for High School boys and girls entering 9th thru 12th grade this fall. It’s a great way to get your players ready for the upcoming fall season. We hope to make this annual event even bigger than last year! All games will be played at one location at the North Coast Premier Soccer Complex at 8809 Lake Road in Seville, Ohio (aka Lodi Soccer Complex). Our massive outdoor soccer complex is the premier soccer destination in northeast Ohio. Our facility is south of Cleveland at I-71 and I-76. Registration DEADLINE is June 20, 2015.

Each team will be guaranteed three 55 minute games. The cost will is $275 per team (boys, girls, varsity or JV).

Additional Details: The Middletown Select Soccer Club is happy to invite you to come and spend the weekend with us at the SPRING BLAST TOURNAMENT. The tournament will be held at Smith Park in Middletown Ohio, and Franklin Community Park in Franklin. Smith park has been home to many tournaments: including the Franchise, State SAY and High School Tournaments. The tournament will offer competition for boys and girls in the U-8 through U-19 brackets. All teams must be in good standing with the United States Soccer Association and only players with valid player passes will be eligible to play. A maximum of 12 players per roster of U8-U9, U10 6v6 division and a maximum of 16 players, 11-U12 8v8 division. A maximum of 18 players per roster will be allowed for U13-U18 11v11.

This year we will offer U10 (8v8) max 12 players and U12 (11v11) max 16 players in both boys and girls. Divisions will be made as long as there are 4 teams to be placed in the schedule

Four (4) guest players will be allowed. No player may play on nor be registered on more than one participating team.

Kolping Seth Stevens Memorial Tournament - Kolping Soccer Club

05/16/2014 - 05/18/2014  -  Cincinnati, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15,U16,U17,U18,U19
Girls: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15,U16,U17,U18,U19

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: Each year our tournament continues to grow. It's not because of the competition that comes out to participate, but because each year teams, families and players understand what our tournament is about. Kolping holds this tournament in order to remember Seth Stevens as a player and a friend. Therefore, we donate a large portion of the tournament proceeds to Children's Hospital Hemotology/Oncology Division where Seth was being Treated.

We also, run a Toy Drive so that we can donate Toys to Children's Hospital as well. Each year we are shocked, surprised, and thankful of all the Donations that Teams, Families, Players and Organizations make. It is great to see all different teams come together for a Great Cause.

Last year we had a great success with the donations. Kids from all clubs raised money, selling lemonade or going door to door asking for donations, just to be able to give toys to the hospital. It was a great success. Please see the about tournament tab to read more about the story of Seth Stevens.

A maximum roster size of 12 players will be permitted for U8, U9 & U10 (6v6); 14 players will be permitted for U11-U12 (8v8). A maximum roster size of 18 players will be permitted for U13-U15 (11v11). Maximum number of guest players for all ages will be four. No player shall be allowed to register with more than one team or switch to another team during the tournament.

Our group of volunteers has given countless hours over the last six months to help make this years MIST our best event ever. We would like to thank them and our many sponsors for their generosity and community support. Without all of these people, the MIST would not be possible.

North Ridgeville Cornfest KickOff - North Ridgeville Amateur Soccer League

08/11/2012 - 08/12/2012  -  North Ridgeville, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15
Girls: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: The North Ridgeville Cornfest KickOff is the perfect opportunity for teams and coaches to make any last minute fine tuning and adjustments to their teams through player positions, formations, plays, etc., before the fall season begins. It provides one last opportunity to make any necessary moves against appropriately bracketed competition.
The tournament is geared toward pleasing the player and coach through great competition, playing games on dedicated soccer fields with white lines, no shortened games or surprising new tournament rules, and adequate space for teams to warm up and prepare for their next game.
In addition to being a player's tournament, the Cornfest Kickoff has not forgotten about the families and supporters of our players. We pride ourselves on providing as many conveniences and amenities as we can to our audience, learning from our own past experiences at other tournaments. Reasonable costs for game fees, souvenirs, and concessions are just one part of that. In addition, we will provide convenient parking, ample bathroom facilities, and lots of entertainment at and outside the tournament, including our famous Corn Festival being held the same weekend!
Our goal is to provide a team/player oriented tournament that promotes sportsmanship and challenge through healthy competition on the soccer field. We are also committed to remembering those who stand by and support these young men and woman in their pursuit of excellence and provide for them as best we can through convenience and courtesy!
We invite you, your team, and your family to join us on August 11th and 12th for the North Ridgeville Cornfest KickOff and experience the difference for yourself!

Additional Details: The Thunder United Metro Futbol Club would like to invite you to join us for our 12th annual adidas Thunder United Classic. This year's tournament will be held the weekend prior to Labor Day weekend, August 25-26th, with local teams possibly playing on Friday evening, August 24th. The Classic is held at Lebanon Sports Complex in Lebanon, Ohio, which can host up to 30 fields at one time, and is centrally located between Cincinnati and Dayton and minutes away from Interstates 75 and 71. Last year's tournament featured a record number of 170 teams in 25 different divisions. It is a great opportunity for teams to gain experience prior to league play beginning.

The tournament will offer competition in the U8-U15 divisions for boys and girls. The U8, U9 and U10 divisions will play 6 a-side, U11 and U12 will play 8 a-side. If possible, multiple divisions will be created in each age group. All divisions will receive champion and finalist team and individual awards. Each participating team will receive a minimum of three games with a final in each division.

The entry fee for the Classic is $375 U8-U10, $425 for U11/U12 and $475 for U13 & U14/15.

Four guest players are permitted per team, but no player can be rostered on more than one team. U14/15 teams may use up to three U15 players that are on the original roster. U15 players are not permitted to play as guest players. (Trapped 8th graders, rostered to a team may play)

We are very proud of our facility and of the tournament and look forward to what is going to be our most successful tournament yet. Please join us for a weekend of soccer and Fun.

Additional Details: You are invited to apply for participation in the 33rd Annual MEAD CUSA CUP Youth Soccer Tournament. The Tournament will be played on September 1 - 3. Team registration will be held Friday, August 31st at the Dayton Marriott Hotel. For those unable to make the registration event on Friday, we offer registration by mail and email - pre-registration details willl be sent with team acceptance notices on or about August 1st.

The primary tournament format calls for three preliminary round games with Semi and Final Matches in each division. (Some divisions may have Quarter Final Matches depending on the number of teams in the division). Some divisions will play a 4-game round robin format. Individual and Team trophies will be awarded for 1st and 2nd places. Semi-Final participants will receive individual medals. Participation awards for U8-U9 teams.

U-8, U-9 and U10 teams will play 6v6, with U-10 teams having the option of playing 8v8. U-11 teams will play 8v8. U-12 teams have the option of playing 8v8 or 11v11. U-13 and U-14 teams will play 11v11. Note that application fees follow the format of play not the age group.

Applicants must be duly registered members of their respective State, Province, or National association. Players must be registered to the team making application. All teams and players accepted to this tournament will be verified. Only players with valid player passes will be permitted to play. See Tournament Rules for more details.

Womens adidas Blue Chip Showcase Tournament - Cincinnati United Soccer League

04/15/2011 - 04/17/2011  -  Cincinnati, Ohio

Gender: Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: 
Girls: U15,U16,U17

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: Hammer FC has been hosting the adidas Blue Chip Showcase Tournament for many years. Through years of hard work and commitment, the event has grown into one of the truly exclusive showcase tournaments for both U-16 and U-17 men and women from around the county. In 2010, approximately 300 college coaches from throughout the United States. Since we stagger the start time of each match, each team’s exposure is enhanced because college coaches can devote their attention to about one half of each match before the next one begins. Thus, a coach does not really have to choose which of several matches starting at the same time to observe. Each team plays only one match per day to help ensure a quality performance.

300+ college coaches attended the 2009 tournament over both weekends and the Hammer FC received numerous compliments from the coaches, and participating teams, regarding the quality of the event and the great effort put forth by the Showcase organizers and support staff.

Archived Website: http://www.classicshammerfc.com/

Midfest Soccer Classic - CUSL

09/24/2011 - 09/25/2011  -  Middletown, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15
Girls: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: The Middletown Select Soccer Club is happy to invite you to come and spend the weekend of Sept 24 & 25, 2011 at the 6th Annual MIDFEST SOCCER CLASSIC TOURNAMENT. The tournament will be held at Smith Park fields in Middletown. Smith park has been home to many tournaments: including the Middletown Spring Blast, SAY Franchise, State SAY and High School Tournaments.

The tournament will offer competition for boys and girls in the U-8 through U-15 brackets. All teams must be in good standing with the United States Soccer Association and only players with valid player passes will be eligible to play. A maximum of 12 players per roster for U8. U9, U10. A maximum of 14 players per roster will be allowed for U11 and U12, a maximum of 18 players for U13-U15. four(4) guest players will be allowed. U8 - U10 will play 6v6, U11 and U12 will play 8v8 all other divisions U13-U15 will play 11 v 11. This year we are offering U12 11v11 play. We will have a division if enough teams apply. Roster size on U12 11v11 will be 18 players. No player may play on nor be registered on more than one participating team. Midfest Soccer Classic Tournament Committee reserves the right of acceptance, denial or placement of any team.

The entry fee of $400.00 for U8-U10 and $425.00 for U11-U15 per team should be mailed along with the enclosed application form to the address listed below by September 1, 2011. Teams not accepted will have their application fee returned in their notification letter. No entry fee will be returned to those teams accepted into the tournament. Notifications will be emailed and posted on the web site by September 10, 2011.

We are very proud of the Soccer facilities at Smith park in Middletown. Smith offer playgrounds, walking trails around the park, refreshment areas and with a total 24 fields for your soccer enjoyment. There are plenty of restaurants and shopping close park. Pets are allowed at Smith park but must be kept on leash. The tournament is set up on a three game format. Individual and team trophies will be awarded for first and second place teams in each division. Trophy's will be awarded after final game at the stage near the tournament headquarters.

Parking will be limited in some areas of the park, so please carpool as mich as possible.

Team registration will be held at the Kingdom Sports Center in Franklin, Ohio on Friday Sept 23, 2011 from 6 pm - 9 pm.

Archived Website: http://www.midfestsoccerclassic.com

Additional Details: This is our 7th year hosting this wonderful tournament. Last year we had a total of 252 teams with 3 states being represented, thus making the Brunswick Classic the largest tournament in North East Ohio four years running. Each team was appropriately bracketed. Competition at each level, age and gender was just fabulous. Everyone had a great time. And we enjoyed hosting all those teams. We had teams from as far as Michigan, Pennsylvania and Canada. We had many teams from the Toledo area, teams from Akron, Bay, Medina, Strongsville, North Royalton, Lakewood, Shaker and Twinsburg just to name a few. All the teams are listed and posted on our website for your viewing. Again, we had a great weekend! Please come and join us in the fun and spirit of competition here in the wonderful City of Brunswick.

Clubs, teams, coaches, players, parents and soccer fans, I personally extend our soccer clubs invitation to come to the fine city of Brunswick and participate in our Classic soccer tournament. Your experience here will be something to remember.

Tournament weekend is November 5 & 6, 2011. Games start early Saturday morning so make sure your teams are ready to go early. Team Registration is Friday, November 4, 2011. All teams must register Friday night, there are no Saturday registrations.

See you all in November. Any questions, please do not hesitate to ask.

Sincerely and Yours in Soccer,
Jeff Petrenko

Womens adidas Blue Chip Showcase Tournament - Cincinnati United Soccer League

04/16/2010 - 04/18/2010  -  Cincinnati, Ohio

Gender: Female    Age Group(s): NULL Boys: 
Girls: U16,U17

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: Classics Hammer FC has been hosting the adidas Blue Chip Showcase Tournament for many years. Through years of hard work and commitment, the event has grown into one of the truly exclusive showcase tournaments for both U-16 and U-17 men and women from around the county. In 2009, it attracted in excess of 300 college coaches from throughout the United States. Since we stagger the start time of each match, each team’s exposure is enhanced because college coaches can devote their attention to about one half of each match before the next one begins. Thus, a coach does not really have to choose which of several matches starting at the same time to observe. Each team plays only one match per day to help ensure a quality performance.

Archived Website: http://www.classicshammerfc.com/

Matthew Kuglics Memorial Tournament - Green Soccer Association

08/13/2010 - 08/15/2010  -  Green, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s): NULL Boys: U10,U11,U12,U13,U14
Girls: U10,U11,U12,U13,U14

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: The Green Soccer Association and the City of Green, Ohio are very proud to announce the newest soccer tournament to be endorsed by OYSAN. At some of the newest and finest facilities in the state, Matthew Kuglics it is a tournament to honor the memory of a local hero, Matthew Kuglics. Air Force Staff Sergeant Kuglics was killed in action by a roadside bomb June 5, 2007 in Kirkuk, Iraq during his seventh year of service and his second tour of duty. Matthew, a 2000 graduate of Green High School, loved soccer, played soccer in high school and continued to play in the Air Force. During his last weekend, his mother said, her son played a soccer game with some of his comrades at his base in Iraq.

Archived Website: http://www.socceronamission.com/kuglics.html

Flag City Classic at Rotary Arena - Findlay Soccer Club

09/24/2010 - 09/26/2010  -  Findlay, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s): NULL Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14
Girls: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: The Flag City Classic is the brain child of one man. That man is Michael Lewis. The dream started with the idea that Findlay needed two premier soccer fields complete with drainage, irrigation, and lights that will allow the children of Hancock County and the surrounding area the opportunity to play on world class fields "Under the Lights" in Prime Time. With the help of the Findlay Rotary, Marathon Oil Company, and Mr. Michael Gardner, this dream has become a reality. With the fields nearing completion Mike realized that these fields gave Findlay the unique opportunity to create a World Class soccer tournament to be played at Rotary Arena.


You see, Mike has spent the last several years taking his two sons to tournaments all over the Tri-State Area. In his travels he often found himself thinking that if he were in charge of a tournament certain things would be different. Things like: better field locations, better restroom facilities, better parking, better hotel accommodations, better restaurants, easier access to hand sanitizer and up to the minute scoring and standings to name a few. Mike knew that in order to pull this off, he would need to assemble a team of leaders like the soccer world had never seen to serve on the FCC committee. With the help of the committee Mike is focusing on these improvements and continues to find new ways to make the Flag City Classic at Rotary Arena the premier Soccer tournament in Ohio!


With all of that being said, possibly the most impressive part of this tournament is that the proceeds will not only go towards Rotary Arena and the Findlay Soccer Club, a portion will also be donated to National and International Relief Projects through Rotary such as supporting a literacy program right here in the United States and digging wells in remote African villages.
With the Flag City Classic’s commitment to making this tournament the best tournament experience your teams and families will ever have and the chance to support worthwhile charitable relief efforts around the world, we hope that you will join us from September 24th through the 26th for the First Annual Flag City Classic at Rotary Arena. See you there!

Archived Website: http://www.flagcityclassic.com/

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: The NOSO Cup International Youth Soccer tournament is hosted by the North Olmstead Soccer Organization, takes place over the July 4th weekend and is played over two days with each team guaranteed 3 games. Many teams use the tournament as a link between the spring and fall sessions – a last get together for teams having completed the spring season, or a first get together for teams competing in the fall. Since 1977, teams from throughout the Midwest and as far away as Florida and Texas have participated. International teams have come from Canada, the United Kingdom, Germany and France.

In addition to the tournament, northern Ohio is home to an exciting lineup of attractions that includes the Rock and Roll Hall of Fame and Cedar Point Amusement Park

Brunswick Fall Classic - Brunswick Soccer Association

11/07/2009 - 11/08/2009  -  Brunswick, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14
Girls: U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: Invitation to Join Us in Brunswick!

Coaches, players, parents and soccer fans a like, come join us in Brunswick, Ohio, and participate in our Fall Classic Soccer Tournament. Our tournament will offer that end of the season competition you have been looking for to compliment your Fall season teams’ efforts and hard work. Brunswick is a great community and extends their city’s hospitality to you. Last year, we were the largest soccer tournament in North East Ohio for the second year in a row with 240 teams participating.

OYSAN Approved

The 2009 Brunswick Classic Soccer Tournament is approved by Ohio Youth Soccer Association North (OYSAN) and is open to all classic, league, premier and tournament teams affiliated with USSF. Teams from outside Ohio North must have approved permission to travel from their state association along with emergency medical forms. Other USSF-affiliated teams, especially those from US Club Soccer, are welcomed to participate, but must bring proof of insurance from USCS, AYSO, SAY or their USSF-affiliated organization. All participating teams will be required to supply coaches and player passes, a copy of their league approved roster and medical release forms. Foreign teams are not accepted.

Format of Play

Our Classic Tournament will be of the traditional youth tournament format. The number of divisions per age group will be based on amount of teams participating. U8 and U9 teams will play 4 games, U10 and older 3 games. Games are two 25 minute halves. Teams will earn 3 points for a win, 1 point for a tie and no points (0) for a loss. Teams with the most points after the 3 games will advance to the championship game. Teams who are tied in points after 3 games will go through the tie breaking rules spelled out in our tournament rules to determine advancement to the championship game. There will be 1st and 2nd place awards for every player in the competitive championship games as well as awards for the teams' coaches. Every U9 and younger player will receive a participative award. There is no championship round for the U8 and U9 teams.

Special note for U8 and U9 teams

Depending on the amount of U8 teams that enter, your team may be placed in an U9 division and bracketed accordingly (meaning your division will consist mostly of U8 and weaker U9 teams). Same goes for U9 teams, your team may be placed in an U10 division and bracketed accordingly. Your entry fees will not be affected by the tournament moving your team to an older division. U8 and U9 teams of course have the option to request to play at an older age group. Please contact the tournament director with any questions or concerns.

Special note for U14 teams

The U14/15 division is named such in the event U14 teams have U15 players on their team. We are not planning on having full U15 aged teams playing in the U14 division. This is basically to allow players who are not playing in high school and are playing with other U14’s. So therefore all the U14 divisions will be named U14/U15. Any questions or concerns on any of these explanations, please contact the tournament director.

Levels of Play

All classic, league, premier and tournament teams are welcomed. Teams will be placed accordingly based on their level of play. Teams may request to be placed in a higher division with the tournament director’s approval. The Brunswick Classic bracketing committee researches your team and places them to their appropriate skill level so we can provide the most competitive while fair tournament challenge for your team.

-1- Entry Fees and Number of Games

The entry fees for this tournament are as follows per team:

U8 teams play 5v5 (with a keeper) $300 (4 games) U9 teams play 6v6 $350 (4 games) U10 teams play 6v6 $350 (3 game minimum) U11-U12 teams play 8v8 $375 (3 game minimum) U13-U14/15 teams play 11v11 $400 (3 game minimum)

This is a rain or shine tournament. In the event some games cannot be played due to unusually bad weather, refunds in the amount of 1/3 the teams' entry fee per game for each unplayed match. The tournament director will determine if a game is to be cancelled due to poor weather conditions. There will be NO REFUNDS for any other reason once a team has been notified of acceptance by depositing your check in the bank. The tournament reserves the right to combine age groups and arrange divisions by format rather than age group; teams will not receive a refund of the tournament entry fee if they withdraw because they do not like the format or bracketing. This tournament does carry a 3-game guarantee.

Team and Player Eligibility

Youth teams properly registered with their state associations and/or USSF affiliates are eligible. All coaches and players must have player pass and/or a copy of their league’s approved roster. Youth rosters are limited to 18 for U13 & U14/15, 14 for U11 & U12's, 12 for U9 & U10's and 10 for U8's. U15 players who are still in 8th grade may play with U14 teams, but no U15 players in high school are permitted. The U15 player’s pass should be enough proof that they are indeed eligible. Guest players are allowed. U8 are permitted 2 guest players, U9 & U10 are permitted 3 and U11 through U14 are allowed 4. Guest players follow the same eligibility rules as the participating players. Teams must present medical authorization or releases at registration for all players. Guest players must be from the same USSF affiliate as the team to which they are requesting to guest play with. Please see the Tournament Rules on guest players so there are no misunderstandings on their eligibility.

Game Schedules and Times

Your team's game schedule will be posted on our website at least one week prior to the tournament. Monitor the website for that schedule. Based on the amount of teams entered will determine how many fields we require, size and format along with the times we will start in the morning. Each team is expected to be ready to play at any time on either day, Saturday and Sunday. So make every effort to have your players here the night before if you are traveling a far distance. We will do our best to accommodate special requests but again, we cannot promise your game schedules will permit you to drive in that morning.

Special Note for Coaches (Please Read)

It is very important that you as coaches have your coaches' passes prior to coming to our tournament. Those coaches' passes must be with your team representative who is registering the team the night before the start of the tournament. Only a registered, carded coach can be on the sidelines with their respective team coaching, no one else in permitted to coach the team. Also, we stress and encourage all teams to have at least 2 coaches per team in the event one of your coaches is unavailable and cannot coach a particular game or that weekend. We have done our best to accommodate scheduling requests but we cannot promise your game schedules will fit your personal schedule. Also, in the event as a coach you coach more than one team entered in the tournament and your teams are scheduled to play at times which make it difficult for you to be in 2 places at once, an assistant or extra coach would solve that problem. In addition, in the event a coach is carded and ineligible to coach the next tournament game, an extra coach is needed here as well. Please make every effort to consider making plans to have more than one registered and carded coach available to coach your teams.

-2- Special Note on Guest Players (Please Read)

It is also very important that you understand the guest player rule. A guest player (someone not on your official and current roster) can only guest for the same USSF affiliated team to which they are requesting to guest play with. For example, an US Youth Soccer team may only have US Youth Soccer players. An US Club team may only have US Club players. If any players want to guest from US Club to US Youth Soccer, they can ONLY by registering with US Youth Soccer and applying for a guest player pass from US Youth Soccer.

Entry Deadline

The entry deadline must be postmarked by Friday, September 25, 2009. Mail entries to P.O. Box 633, Brunswick, Ohio 44212, to the attention of Jeff Petrenko, Tournament Director. Be sure to include your check. No entry is accepted until paid in full. Any and all questions and comments can be entertained by emailing the tournament director at jap0711@aol.com, please include "tournament questions" in the email’s subject line.

Final Comments

A tournament package will be made available on the tournament's website. Included on the website will be a welcome letter, your team’s game schedule, the tournament rules, team roster form, registration dates, location and requirements, site field maps and directions, a medical release form (teams can use their own), FAQ’s and any additional information as required to make your tournament experience a memorable one.

Additional information regarding the tournament’s format can be found in our tournament rules. Please visit our website to access those rules.

This is our 5th year hosting this wonderful tournament. Last year we had a total of 240 teams with 3 states being represented, thus making the Brunswick Classic the largest tournament in North East Ohio two years running. Each team was appropriately bracketed. Competition at each level, age and gender was just fabulous. Everyone had a great time. And we enjoyed hosting all those teams. We had teams from as far as Michigan and Pennsylvania. We had many teams from the Toledo area, teams from Akron, Findlay, North Royalton, Lakewood and Twinsburg just to name a few. All the teams are listed and posted on our website for your viewing. Again, we had a great weekend! Please come and join us in the fun and spirit of competition here in the wonderful City of Brunswick.

Clubs, teams, coaches, players, parents and soccer fans, I personally extend our soccer club’s invitation to come to the fine city of Brunswick and participate in our Classic soccer tournament. Your experience here will be something to remember.

Tournament weekend is November 7 & 8, 2009. Games start Saturday morning. Team Registration is Friday, November 6, 2009. All teams must register Friday night, there are no Saturday registrations.

See you all in November. Any questions, please do not hesitate to ask.

Sincerely and Yours in Soccer, Jeff Petrenko Tournament Director 2009 Brunswick Fall Classic www.eteamz.com/brunswicksoccerasc

Archived Website: http://eteamz.com/brunswicksoccerasc

Brunswick Fall Classic - Brunswick Soccer Association

11/08/2008 - 11/09/2008  -  Brunswick, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14
Girls: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: 2008 BRUNSWICK CLASSIC SOCCER TOURNAMENT

Invitation to Join Us in Brunswick!

Coaches, players, parents and soccer fans a like, come join us in Brunswick, Ohio, and participate in our Fall Classic Soccer Tournament. Our tournament will offer that end of the season competition you have been looking for to compliment your Fall season teams’ efforts and hard work. Brunswick is a great community and extends their city’s hospitality to you. Last year, we were the largest soccer tournament in North East Ohio with 238 teams participating and 5 states being represented.

OYSAN Approved

The 2008 Brunswick Classic Soccer Tournament is approved by Ohio Youth Soccer Association North (OYSAN) and is open to all classic, league, premier and tournament teams affiliated with USSF. Teams from outside Ohio North must have approved permission to travel from their state association along with notarized emergency medical forms. Other USSF-affiliated teams, especially those from US Club Soccer, are welcomed to participate, but must bring proof of insurance from USCS, AYSO, SAY or their USSF-affiliated organization. All participating teams will be required to supply coaches and player passes, a copy of their league approved roster and medical release forms. Foreign teams are not accepted.

Format of Play

Our Classic Tournament will be of the traditional youth tournament format. The number of divisions per age group will be based on amount of teams participating. U8 and U9 teams will play 4 games, U10 and older 3 games. Games are two 25 minute halves. Teams will earn 3 points for a win, 1 point for a tie and no points (0) for a loss. Teams with the most points after the 3 games will advance to the championship game. Teams who are tied in points after 3 games will go through the tie breaking rules spelled out in our tournament rules to determine advancement to the championship game. There will be 1st and 2nd place awards for every player in the competitive championship games as well as awards for the teams' coaches. Every U9 and younger player will receive a participative award. There is no championship round for the U8 and U9 teams.

Levels of Play

All classic, league, premier and tournament teams are welcomed. Teams will be placed accordingly based on their level of play. Teams may request to be placed in a higher division with the tournament director’s approval. The Brunswick Classic bracketing committee researches your team and places them to their appropriate skill level so we can provide the most competitive while fair tournament challenge for your team.

Entry Fees and Number of Games

The entry fees for this tournament are as follows per team:

U8 teams play 5v5 $300 (4 games)
U9 teams play 6v6 $300 (4 games)
U10 teams play 6v6 $325 (3 game minimum)
U11-U12 teams play 8v8 $350 (3 game minimum)
U13-U14 teams play 11v11 $350 (3 game minimum)

This is a rain or shine tournament. In the event some games cannot be played due to unusually bad weather, refunds in the amount of 1/3 the teams' entry fee per game for each unplayed match. The tournament director will determine if a game is to be cancelled due to poor weather conditions. There will be NO REFUNDS for any other reason once a team has been notified of acceptance by depositing your check in the bank. The tournament reserves the right to combine age groups and arrange divisions by format rather than age group; teams will not receive a refund of the tournament entry fee if they withdraw because they do not like the format or bracketing. This tournament does carry a 3-game guarantee.

Team and Player Eligibility

Youth teams properly registered with their state associations and/or USSF affiliates are eligible. All coaches and players must have player pass and/or a copy of their league’s approved roster. Youth rosters are limited to 18 for U13 & U14/15, 14 for U11 & U12's, 12 for U9 & U10's and 10 for U8's. U15 players who are still in 8th grade may play with U14 teams, but no U15 players in high school are permitted. The U15 player’s pass should be enough proof that they are indeed eligible. Guest players are allowed. U8 are permitted 2 guest players, U9 & U10 are permitted 3 and U11 through U14 are allowed 4. Guest players follow the same eligibility rules as the participating players. Teams must present medical authorization or releases at registration for all players. Guest players must be from the same USSF affiliate as the team to which they are requesting to guest play with. Please see the Tournament Rules on guest players so there are no misunderstandings on their eligibility.

Game Schedules and Times

Your team's game schedule will be posted on our website at least one week prior to the tournament. Monitor the website for that schedule. Based on the amount of teams entered will determine how many fields we require, size and format along with the times we will start in the morning. Each team is expected to be ready to play at any time on either day, Saturday and Sunday. So make every effort to have your players here the night before if you are traveling a far distance. We will do our best to accommodate special requests but again, we cannot promise your game schedules will permit you to drive in that morning.

Special Note for Coaches (Please Read)

It is very important that you as coaches have your coaches' passes prior to coming to our tournament. Those coaches' passes must be with your team representative who is registering the team the night before the start of the tournament. Only a registered, carded coach can be on the sidelines with their respective team coaching, no one else in permitted to coach the team. Also, we stress and encourage all teams to have at least 2 coaches per team in the event one of your coaches is unavailable and cannot coach a particular game or that weekend. We have done our best to accommodate scheduling requests but we cannot promise your game schedules will fit your personal schedule. Also, in the event as a coach you coach more than one team entered in the tournament and your teams are scheduled to play at times which make it difficult for you to be in 2 places at once, an assistant or extra coach would solve that problem. In addition, in the event a coach is carded and ineligible to coach the next tournament game, an extra coach is needed here as well. Please make every effort to consider making plans to have more than one registered and carded coach available to coach your teams.

Special Note on Guest Players (Please Read)

It is also very important that you understand the guest player rule. A guest player (someone not on your official and current roster) can only guest for the same USSF affiliated team to which they are requesting to guest play with. For example, an Ohio North team (OYSAN) may only have Ohio North players. A US Club team may only have US Club players. If any players want to guest from US Club to Ohio North, they can ONLY by registering with Ohio North (becoming a member) and applying for a guest player pass from Ohio North.

Entry Deadline

The entry deadline must be postmarked by Saturday, September 27, 2008. Mail entries to P.O. Box 633, Brunswick, Ohio 44212, to the attention of Jeff Petrenko, Tournament Director. Be sure to include your check. No entry is accepted until paid in full. Any and all questions and comments can be entertained by emailing the tournament director at jap0711@aol.com, please include "tournament questions" in the letter’s subject line.

Final Comments

A tournament package will be made available on the tournament's website. Included on the website will be a welcome letter, your team’s game schedule, the tournament rules, team roster form, registration dates, location and requirements, site field maps and directions, a medical release form (teams can use their own) and any additional information as required to make your tournament experience a memorable one.

Additional information regarding the tournament’s format can be found in our tournament rules. Please visit our website to access those rules.

This is our 4th year hosting this wonderful tournament. Last year we had a total of 238 teams with 5 states being represented, thus making the Brunswick Classic the largest tournament in North East Ohio last year. Each team was appropriately bracketed. Competition at each level, age and gender was just great. Everyone had a great time. And we had a great time hosting all those teams. We had teams from as far as Michigan, West Virginia, Kentucky and Pennsylvania. We had many teams from the Toledo area, teams from Akron, North Royalton, Lakewood and Twinsburg just to name a few. Our local, neighboring communities such as Medina and Strongsville sent over 20 teams each to our tournament. All the teams are listed and posted on our website for your viewing. Again, we had a great weekend and the weather cooperated again! Please come and join us in the fun and spirit of competition here in the wonderful City of Brunswick.

Clubs, teams, coaches, players, parents and soccer fans, I personally extend our soccer club’s invitation to come to the fine city of Brunswick and participate in our Classic soccer tournament. Your experience here will be something to remember.

Tournament weekend is November 8 & 9, 2008. Games start Saturday morning. Team Registration is Friday, November 7, 2008. All teams must register Friday night, no Saturday registrations.

See you all then.

Sincerely and Yours in Soccer, Jeff Petrenko Tournament Director 2008 Brunswick Classic www.brunswicksoccerasc.com

Anderson's Army Soccer Challenge - 6v6 Soccer Challenge

05/19/2007 - 05/20/2007  -  Grove City, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: Mens Open
Girls: Womens Open

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: 3rd Annual Anderson's Army Soccer Challenge will be held in Central, Ohio (site TBA) on May 19th and 20th. This year we have teamed up with the Anderson's Army to "fight the beast". This years tournament is a tribute to our friend who lost his fight to Melanomo in 2004. Brian loved this game and it is why we are so proud to team up with the Anderson's Army group to raise awareness and raise funds for research. This years tournament will be coupled with a player check in party, player giveaways, and the Columbus Crew Caravan will be in attendance.

Tournaments feature the following divisions: • Men’s: Open, B, 30+, 40+ • Women’s: Open, B, 30+ • Co-ed: Open & Rec.

The 6 V 6 Soccer Challenge game is played on a 60 x 40 yard pitch with a size 4 ball and no offside. Goal sizes are 6 x 12 feet. Rosters are limited to 10 players. Co-ed games require two females on the field at all times.

This format offers players an intense, fast-paced game that features end-to-end action with plenty of scoring opportunities. Tournament weekends includes a three-game guarantee, players’ party with discount food and drink specials, plus a host hotel for traveling teams.

Brunswick Fall Classic - Brunswick Soccer Association

11/03/2007 - 11/04/2007  -  Brunswick, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14
Girls: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: 2007 BRUNSWICK CLASSIC SOCCER TOURNAMENT Invitation to Join Us in Brunswick November 3rd and 4th, 2007! Coaches, players, parents and soccer fans a like, come join us in Brunswick, Ohio, and participate in our Fall Classic Soccer Tournament. Our tournament will offer that end of the season competition you have been looking for to compliment your Fall season teams’ efforts and hard work. Brunswick is a great community and extends their city’s hospitality to you. OYSAN Approved The 2007 Brunswick Classic Soccer Tournament is approved by Ohio Youth Soccer Association North (OYSAN) and is open to all classic, league, premier and tournament teams affiliated with USSF. Teams from outside Ohio North must have approved permission to travel from their state association along with notarized emergency medical forms. Other USSF-affiliated teams, especially those from US Club Soccer, are welcomed to participate, but must bring proof of insurance from USCS, AYSO, SAY or their USSF-affiliated organization. All participating teams will be required to supply coaches and player passes, a copy of their league approved roster and medical release forms. Foreign teams are not accepted. Format of Play Our Classic Tournament will be of the traditional youth tournament format. The number of divisions per age group will be based on amount of teams participating. U8 and U9 teams will play 4 games, U10 and older 3 games. Games are two 25 minute halves. Teams will earn 3 points for a win, 1 point for a tie and no points (0) for a loss. Teams with the most points after the 3 games will advance to the championship game. Teams who are tied in points after 3 games will go through the tie breaking rules spelled out in our tournament rules to determine advancement to the championship game. There will be 1st and 2nd place awards for every player in the competitive championship games as well as awards for the teams' coaches. Every U9 and younger player will receive a participative award. There is no championship round for the U8 and U9 teams. Levels of Play All classic, league, premier and tournament teams are welcomed. Teams will be placed accordingly based on their level of play. Teams may request to be placed in a higher division with the tournament director’s approval. The Brunswick Classic bracketing committee researches your team and places them to their appropriate skill level so we can provide the most competitive while fair tournament challenge for your team. Entry Fees and Number of Games The entry fees for this tournament are as follows per team: U8 teams play 5v5 $250 (4 games) U9 teams play 6v6 $275 (4 games) U10 teams play 6v6 $300 (3 game minimum) U11-U12 teams play 8v8 $325 (3 game minimum) U13-U14 teams play 11v11 $350 (3 game minimum) This is a rain or shine tournament. In the event some games cannot be played due to unusually bad weather, refunds in the amount of 1/3 the teams' entry fee per game for each unplayed match. The tournament director will determine if a game is to be cancelled due to poor weather conditions. There will be NO REFUNDS for any other reason once a team has been notified of acceptance by depositing your check in the bank. The tournament reserves the right to combine age groups and arrange divisions by format rather than age group; teams will not receive a refund of the tournament entry fee if they withdraw because they do not like the format or bracketing. This tournament does carry a 3-game guarantee. Team and Player Eligibility Youth teams properly registered with their state associations and/or USSF affiliates are eligible. All coaches and players must have player pass and/or a copy of their league’s approved roster. Youth rosters are limited to 18 for U13 and U14/15, U11 and U12 to 14 and U10 and younger are 12. U15 players who are still in 8th grade may play with U14 teams, but no U15 players in high school are permitted. The U15 player’s pass should be enough proof that they are indeed eligible. Guest players are allowed. U8 are permitted 2 guest players, U9 and U10 are permitted 3 and U11 through U14 are allowed 4. Guest players follow the same eligibility rules as the participating players. Teams must present medical authorization or releases at registration for all players. Guest players must be from the same USSF affiliate as the team to which they are requesting to guest play with. Please see the Tournament Rules on guest players so there are no misunderstandings on their eligibility. Game Schedules and Times Your team's game schedule will be posted on our website at least one week prior to the tournament. Monitor the website for that schedule. Based on the amount of teams entered will determine how many fields we require, size and format along with the times we will start in the morning. Each team is expected to be ready to play at any time on either day, Saturday and Sunday. So make every effort to have your players here the night before if you are traveling a far distance. We will do our best to accommodate special requests but again, we cannot promise your game schedules will permit you to drive in that morning. Tournament Weekend and Day Light Savings This particular weekend, November 3rd and 4th, is the weekend the time is changed for day light savings. Fortunately, on Sunday, if you forgot, you will be there one hour too early instead of being late and missing your first Sunday game. This is just a reminder to consider the time change and alert your parents. But not telling them is not a bad thing since again, they will be early rather than late. Chuckle Chuckle :) Special Note for Coaches (Please Read) It is very important that you as coaches have your coaches' passes prior to coming to our tournament. Those coaches' passes must be with your team representative who is registering the team the night before the start of the tournament. Only a registered, carded coach can be on the sidelines with their respective team coaching, no one else in permitted to coach the team. Also, we stress and encourage all teams to have at least 2 coaches per team in the event one of your coaches is unavailable and cannot coach a particular game or that weekend. We have done our best to accommodate scheduling requests but we cannot promise your game schedules will fit your personal schedule. Also, in the event as a coach you coach more than one team entered in the tournament and your teams are scheduled to play at times which make it difficult for you to be in 2 places at once, an assistant or extra coach would solve that problem. In addition, in the event a coach is carded and ineligible to coach the next tournament game, an extra coach is needed here as well. Please make every effort to consider making plans to have more than one registered and carded coach available to coach your teams. Entry Deadline The entry deadline is September 29, 2007. Mail entries to P.O. Box 633, Brunswick, Ohio 44212, to the attention of Jeff Petrenko, Tournament Director. Be sure to include your check. No entry is accepted until paid in full. Any and all questions and comments can be entertained by emailing the tournament director at jap0711@aol.com, please include "tournament questions" in the letter’s subject line. Final Comments A tournament package will be made available on the tournament's website. Included on the website will be a welcome letter, your team’s game schedule, the tournament rules, team roster form, registration dates, location and requirements, site field maps and directions, a medical release form (teams can use their own) and any additional information as required to make your tournament experience a memorable one. Additional information regarding the tournament’s format can be found in our tournament rules. Please visit our website to access those rules. This is our third year hosting this wonderful tournament. Last year we had 187 teams, up 80 from our first year. Each team was appropriately bracketed. Competition at each level, age and gender was just great. Everyone had a great time. And we had a great time hosting all those teams. We had teams from as far as Michigan, West Virginia and Pennsylvania. We had many teams from the Toledo area, teams from Cincinnati, Akron, North Royalton and Twinsburg just to name a few. Our local, neighboring communities such as Medina and Strongsville sent over 20 teams each to our tournament. All the teams are listed and posted on our website for your viewing. Again, we had a great weekend. Please come and join us in the fun and spirit of competition here in the wonderful City of Brunswick. Clubs, teams, coaches, players, parents and soccer fans, I personally extend our soccer club’s invitation to come to the fine city of Brunswick and participate in our Classic soccer tournament. Your experience here will be something to remember. Sincerely and Yours in Soccer, Jeff Petrenko Tournament Director 2007 Brunswick Classic www.brunswicksoccerasc.com

Archived Website: http://www.brunswicksoccerasc.com

Queen City Memorial Day Tournament - Westside Soccer Club

05/27/2006 - 05/29/2006  -  Cincinnati, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s): U9-17, 19 B/G Boys: U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15,U16,U17,U18,U19U9,U10,U11,U12,U13
Girls: U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14,U15,U16,U17,U19

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details:

Whether you join us every Memorial Day, or simply want to start being a part of the tradition, apply to the Queen City Tournament knowing we promise some of the best competitive soccer in the region! Last year we featured over 300 teams from Ohio South, Ohio North, Kentucky, Indiana, Pennsylvania, Michigan, Missouri, Illinois, West Virginia, Tennessee, Washington DC and New York. What a great way to spend the holiday weekend!

Our tournament is designed to be competitive for ALL teams!

We want your team(s) to enjoy the benefits of playing where they can be the most competitive! Thus, the tournament will have upper and lower divisions for ages 9 through 14 and will attempt this for older age groups as participation allows. Jarosi/Willis Memorial Cup - COSA

06/10/2006 - 06/11/2006  -  Columbus, Ohio

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details: Frank Jarosi died in 1985 of injuries four months after being stuck by lightning during a State Cup tournament. The inception of the Frank Jarosi Memorial Soccer Tournament in 1986 was the result of a wish for a lasting tribute from the Central Ohio Soccer Association. In 1995, the tournament's name was changed to the Jarosi-Willis Memorial Soccer Tournament to also serve as a memorial to Mick Willis, who served as MOSSL President and Jarosi Tournament Director from 1987 to 1995. The tournament has since grown to over 300 teams annually.

Brunswick Classic - Brunswick Soccer Association

11/04/2006 - 11/05/2006  -  Brunswick, Ohio

Gender: Male and Female    Age Group(s):  Boys: U8,U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14
Girls: U9,U10,U11,U12,U13,U14

Facility Type: Outdoor

Additional Details:

2006 BRUNSWICK CLASSIC SOCCER TOURNAMENT

Invitation to Join Us in Brunswick!

Coaches, players, parents and soccer fans a like, come join us in Brunswick, Ohio, and participate in our Fall Classic Soccer Tournament. Our tournament will offer that end of the season competition you have been looking to compliment your Fall season teams’ efforts and hard work. Brunswick is a great community and extends their city’s hospitality to you.

OYSAN Approved

The 2006 Brunswick Classic Soccer Tournament is approved by Ohio Youth Soccer Association North (OYSAN) and is open to all classic, league and premier teams affiliated with USSF. Teams from outside Ohio North must have approved permission to travel from their state association along with notarized emergency medical forms. Other USSF-affiliated teams, especially those from US Club Soccer, are welcomed to participate, but must bring proof of insurance from USCS, AYSO, SAY or their USSF-affiliated organization. All participating teams will be required to supply coaches and player passes, a copy of their league approved roster and medical release forms. Foreign teams are not accepted.

Format of Play

Our Classic Tournament will be of the traditional youth tournament format. The number of divisions per age group will be based on amount of teams participating. Each team will play 3 games. Games are two 25 minute halves. Teams will earn 3 points for a win, 1 point for a tie and no points (0) for a loss. Teams with the most points after the 3 games will advance to the championship game. Teams who are tied in points after 3 games will go through the tie breaking rules spelled out in our tournament rules to determine advancement to the championship game. There will be 1st and 2nd place awards for every player in the competitive championship games as well as awards for the teams' coaches. Every U9 and younger player will receive a participative award.

Levels of Play

All classic, league, premier and tournament teams are welcomed. Teams will be placed accordingly based on their level of play. Teams may request to be placed in a higher division with the tournament director’s approval.

Entry Fees and Number of Games

The entry fees for this tournament are as follows per team:

U8 boys play 4v4 $225 (4 games) U9 teams play 6v6 $250 (4 games) U10 teams play 6v6 $275 (3 game minimum) U11-U12 teams play 8v8 $300 (3 game minimum) U13-U14 teams play 11v11 $325 (3 game minimum)

This is a rain or shine tournament. In the event some games cannot be played due to unusually bad weather, refunds in the amount of 1/3 the teams' entry fee per game for each unplayed match. The tournament director will determine if a game is to be cancelled due to poor weather conditions. There will be NO REFUNDS for any other reason once a team has been notified of acceptance by depositing your check in the bank. The tournament reserves the right to combine age groups and arrange divisions by format rather than age group; teams will not receive a refund of the tournament entry fee if they withdraw because they do not like the format or bracketing. This tournament does carry a 3-game guarantee.

Archived Website: http://www.brunswicksoccerasc.com/
